  <script>
    
    function dispEx(exhibID) {
      
      var dispExPage = "/V40/exhibitor_list/displayEx.cvn?exbid="+exhibID;
      var dispExWidth = 800;
      var dispExHeight = 600;
      
        dispExWidth = 800;
      
        dispExHeight = 600;
      
      var w = 480, h = 340;
      if (document.all || document.layers) {
         w = screen.availWidth;
         h = screen.availHeight;
      }
      var leftPos = (w-dispExWidth)/2, topPos = (h-dispExHeight)/2;

      
        popup=window.open(dispExPage+"&printfr=true&popup=1", "dispExPopup", "width="+dispExWidth+", height="+dispExHeight+", location=no, menubar=no, status=no, toolbar=no, scrollbars=yes, resizable=yes, statusbar=no" + ",top=" + topPos + ",left=" + leftPos);
        popup.focus();
      
    }
  </script>
